TABLE: ALLOTMENT$DETAIL
R&A FAMILY: Bookings
R&A MODULE (schema file): BookingsBlock.graphql
REQUEST TYPE (Query field): bookingsBlock
ENDPOINT: /rna/v1/graphql/

========================
GRAPHQL QUERY
========================
query bookingsBlockForALLOTMENTDETAIL($limit: Int, $offset: Int, $input: BookingsBlockQueryArgumentsType!) {
  bookingsBlock(limit: $limit, offset: $offset, input: $input) {
    blockDetails {
      allotmentType
    }
    blockDetailDetails {
      allotmentHeaderId
      cPickupRate1
      cPickupRate2
      cPickupRate3
      cPickupRate4
      roomCategory
      scRoomCategory
      elasticSold
    }
    eventRevenueDetails {
      forecastRevenue
    }
    sellMessagesDetails {
      sellId
    }
  }
}

========================
VARIABLES (JSON)
========================
{
  "input": {
    "allotmentDetailsResort": {
        "_eq":"{{inputs.hotel_id}}"
    },
    "allotmentDetailsBeginDate":  {
      "_gte": "2021-05-31"
    },
    "allotmentDetailsEndDate":  {
      "_lte": "2026-04-01"
    }
  }
}
